      <li class="menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-has-children menu-item-321" id="menu-item-321">

    <div class="content-sidebar-wrap">
     <main class="content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog" role="main">
      <article class="post-4639 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-25-things-to-sew category-freediybagtutorialsandpatterns category-craftprojectideasandtutorials category-favorite-posts category-sewing-patterns tag-patterns tag-sewing-patterns-2 tag-tutorials entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         Ipad Sleeve Case Tutorial &amp; 25 Things to Sew for your Gadgets
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2013-09-10T06:00:23+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          September 10, 2013
         </time>
         By
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/author/clp" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Amber
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <span class="martiniboy_social_list">
         <ul class="jamie_social martinileft">
          <li class="martinifb">
           <fb:like href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2013/09/ipad-sleeve-case-tutorial-25-things-to-sew-for-your-gadgets-giveaway.html" layout="button_count" send="false" show_faces="false" width="90">
           </fb:like>
          </li>
          <!--[if !lte IE 7]&gt;&lt;!-->
          <li>
           <g:plusone callback="plusone_vote" href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2013/09/ipad-sleeve-case-tutorial-25-things-to-sew-for-your-gadgets-giveaway.html" size="medium">
           </g:plusone>
          </li>
          <!--&lt;![endif]-->
          <li>
           <a class="twitter-share-button" data-count="horizontal" data-text="Ipad Sleeve Case Tutorial &amp; 25 Things to Sew for your Gadgets" data-url="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2013/09/ipad-sleeve-case-tutorial-25-things-to-sew-for-your-gadgets-giveaway.html" href="https://twitter.com/share">
            Tweet
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="pin">
           <a always-show-count="1" class="pin-it-button" count-layout="horizontal" href="http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://crazylittleprojects.com/2013/09/ipad-sleeve-case-tutorial-25-things-to-sew-for-your-gadgets-giveaway.html">
            Pin It
           </a>
           <a class="pinarea" href="javascript:void(run_pinmarklet())">
           </a>
          </li>
          <script src="http://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js" type="text/javascript">
          </script>
         </ul>
         <br class="jamie_clear"/>
        </span>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         As I sit here writing this post Ive got a laptop next to me so that I can watch my favorite show on it while I type my post on my desktop and my husband can borrow my iPad, but someone might text me on my cell phone. You get what I am saying. Lifes full of gadgets these days!
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         So, in honor of National Sewing Month I thought it would be fun to pull together a post with
         <strong>
          25 Things to Sew for Your Gadgets
         </strong>
         . But first I am going to show you an
         <strong>
          iPad Sleeve Case tutorial
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleevecasetutorial.png">
          <img alt="Ipad Case Tutorial by Crazy Little Projects" class="aligncenter" height="639" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleevecasetutorial.png" width="428"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         And guess what? Its got a cute little fabric flower on it!
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ipadcasetutorial.png">
          <img alt="Ipad Sleeve Tutorial and Pattern by Crazy Little Projects" class="aligncenter" height="641" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ipadcasetutorial.png" width="429"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         This is pretty easy to make and would make a really great gift!
        </p>
        <h3 style="text-align: left;">
         <strong>
          <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
           iPad Sleeve Case Tutorial:
          </span>
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Supplies Needed:
         </strong>
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          1/2 yard each of 2 coordinating fabrics
         </li>
         <li>
          1/2 yard of
          <a href="http://www.shareasale.com/r.cfm?u=771742&amp;b=477359&amp;m=46996&amp;afftrack=&amp;urllink=www%2Ethermowebonline%2Ecom%2Fp%2Fheatnbond%2Dfleece%2Dfusible%2Dhigh%2Dloft%2Dwhite%2D45%2Din%2Dd%2Df%2Dx%2Dby%2Dthe%2Dyard" target="_blank">
           fusible fleece
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          Small piece of velcro
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         Before I teach you how, I want to tell you a little bit about my fabric choices. I got these 2 fabrics from
         <a href="http://modernyardage.com/" target="_blank">
          Modern Yardage fabric
         </a>
         . Modern Yardage is a fabric store unlike any you have ever experienced. They actually print their own fabric and so it comes with a wide sidebar where youll find info about bloggers or other sewers, pattern pieces and other fun things:
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Modernyardage.png">
          <img alt="Modernyardage" class="aligncenter" height="644" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Modernyardage.png" width="431"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         And their fabric options are fun and modern and fresh, very unlike what you will find in other fabric stores.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Instructions:
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Cutting guide: Cut 1 of each of the following pieces from each fabric and fusible fleece. (So 3 pieces total of each.)
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          One piece that is 9 inches by 11 inches
         </li>
         <li>
          One piece that is 9 inches by 15 inches
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         If you would like to add the ruffle and the flower, cut the following pieces:
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          One 45 inch long piece that is about 2 inches wide
         </li>
         <li>
          One piece that is 18 inches long by 5 inches wide
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         Lets start with the ruffle. With right sides together, sew along the long side:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Theruffle.png">
          <img alt="Theruffle" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4688" height="427" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Theruffle.png" width="637"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Then turn right side out and press so that the seam is in the center of the back:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/makeanipadcover.png">
          <img alt="makeanipadcover" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4689" height="427" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/makeanipadcover.png" width="637"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Next, run a
         <a href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2012/12/sewing-dictionary-with-pictures.html">
          baste
         </a>
         stitch right down the center:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Gatheringstitc.png">
          <img alt="Gatheringstitc" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4690" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Gatheringstitc.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         And pull gently on the bobbin thread to gather the fabric into a ruffle. Once you have it the length you need it, pin it in place and sew it down the center of your 9 by 11 inch piece of front fabric.
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ruffledipadcase.png">
          <img alt="Ruffledipadcase" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4691" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ruffledipadcase.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
         There are tons of fabric flower tutorials out there, so you can choose one, but
         <a href="http://www.marthastewart.com/americanmade/nominee/81687" target="_blank">
          this is the one I used
         </a>
         , but I did it the reverse way that she describes so that it is not frayed on the edges.
        </p>
        <p>
         Now, before we do anything else, lets add the Velcro. Let me tell you that I discovered as I was making mine that I had no Velcro in the house. So I dont have pictures of where to place this. BUT, you need to place it on the 9 by 11 inch OUTER piece (the one that you just sewed in the center OR you can do two-one near each edge-and then match it up with the INNER piece that is 9 inches by 13 inches. You are sewing both of these on the right side of the fabric and need to do sew them so that they will match up when the flap is folded down. Sorry for the lack of pictures!
        </p>
        <p>
         With your Velcro in place, iron your fusible fleece to your inner pieces. Iron it so that it is on the back side of the fabric.
        </p>
        <p>
         Now, with right sides together sew the 2 outer pieces together and the 2 inner pieces together:
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ipadcasepattern.png">
          <img alt="Ipadcasepattern" class="aligncenter" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Ipadcasepattern.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Now, turn the outer one right side out:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/kindlecase.png">
          <img alt="kindlecase" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4678" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/kindlecase.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         And slide it down into the inner piece:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleevetutorial.png">
          <img alt="ipadsleevetutorial" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4679" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleevetutorial.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         Now, this is the part that always confuses people. We are going to sew from the top flap, around the side, across the middle (but only catching the 9 by 11 inch pieces) and up the other side, leaving several inches to turn it right side out:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/howtosewanipadcase.png">
          <img alt="howtosewanipadcase" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4680" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/howtosewanipadcase.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         Here it is done:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleeve.png">
          <img alt="ipadsleeve" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4681" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadsleeve.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         Then, reach inside and pull out the inner fabric:
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadcasesleeve.png">
          <img alt="ipadcasesleeve" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4682" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/ipadcasesleeve.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Howtomakeanipadcase.png">
          <img alt="Howtomakeanipadcase" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4683" height="434" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Howtomakeanipadcase.png" width="648"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         and tuck the inner fabric down in. Then press it all flat and top stitch the same spot that you just sewed-around the flap and across the center-this will close the opening.
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         Then, hand stitch your flower in place and youre done!
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Flower.png">
          <img alt="Flower" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4692" height="425" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Flower.png" width="635"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <br style="text-align: left;"/>
         <script src="//d12vno17mo87cx.cloudfront.net/embed/rafl/cptr.js" type="text/javascript">
         </script>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: left;">
         Now, lets talk about other things you can sew for your gadgets shall we?
        </p>
        <h3 style="text-align: left;">
         <strong>
          <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
           25 Things to Sew for Your Gadgets:
          </span>
         </strong>
        </h3>
        <p>
         <a href="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/25thingstosewforyourgadgets1.png">
          <img alt="25 Things to Sew for Your Gadgets" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4696" height="802" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/25thingstosewforyourgadgets1.png" width="352"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://erinerickson.com/2010/10/easy-iphone-sleeve-tutorial/" target="_blank">
          Easy iPhone Sleeve
         </a>
         by Erin Erickson:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://erinerickson.com/2010/10/easy-iphone-sleeve-tutorial/" target="_blank">
          <img alt="iPhone Sleeve" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4640" height="240" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Iphonecase.jpg" width="240"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.my3monsters.com/2013/05/diy-iphone-wallet-tutorial.html" target="_blank">
          iPhone Wallet
         </a>
         by My 3 Monsters:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.my3monsters.com/2013/05/diy-iphone-wallet-tutorial.html" target="_blank">
          <img alt="iphonewallet" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-4654" height="202" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/iphonewallet-300x202.jpg" width="300"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.mesewcrazy.com/2013/08/running-belt-diy.html" target="_blank">
          Running Belt for Your Ipod
         </a>
         at The Sewing Rabbit:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.mesewcrazy.com/2013/08/running-belt-diy.html" target="_blank">
          <img alt="Sewbon_Running_Belt_1" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-4656" height="200" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Sewbon_Running_Belt_1-300x200.jpg" width="300"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         Use this
         <a href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2012/09/messenger-bag-tutorial.html">
          Messenger Bag as a Laptop Bag
         </a>
         by Crazy Little Projects:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/2012/09/messenger-bag-tutorial.html">
          <img alt="Messenger Bag Tutorial and Pattern by CrazyLittleProjects.com" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-3335" height="300" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/09/Messengerbagpatternandtutorial-198x300.png" width="198"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.themotherhuddle.com/tutorial-how-to-make-a-custom-laptop-bag/" target="_blank">
          Laptop Bag
         </a>
         by The Mother Huddle:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.themotherhuddle.com/tutorial-how-to-make-a-custom-laptop-bag/" target="_blank">
          <img alt="Laptop Bag" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-4641" height="199" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Laptopbag-300x199.jpg" width="300"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://sewplicity.blogspot.com/2011/09/tutorial-dslr-camera-lens-case.html" target="_blank">
          A Bag for your Camera Lense
         </a>
         by Sewplicity:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://sewplicity.blogspot.com/2011/09/tutorial-dslr-camera-lens-case.html" target="_blank">
          <img alt="Lensebag" class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-4644" height="300" src="http://cf.crazylittleprojects.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/Lensebag-198x300.jpg" width="198"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://www.notjustahousewife.net/2011/02/sew-with-me-saturday-ipod-or-phone-case.html" target="_blank">
          Ipod OR iPhone Case
         </a>
         by Not Just a Housewife:
        </p>

      <section class="widget user-profile" id="user-profile-2">
       <div class="widget-wrap">
        <h4 class="widget-title widgettitle">
         Well hello!
        </h4>
        <p>
         <span class="alignleft">
          <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-65 photo" height="65" src="http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/022845357b2f1a9e08bb8b10d5bcf685?s=65&amp;d=http%3A%2F%2F0.gravatar.com%2Favatar%2Fad516503a11cd5ca435acc9bb6523536%3Fs%3D65&amp;r=G" width="65"/>
         </span>
         Hi! I am Amber. I'm first and foremost a mom to 4 boys. When I am not being a mom or a wife I love to bake, I love to sew, I love to read and I don't like to sit still. Welcome to Crazy Little Projects where I show off my latest crazy projects and show you how you can do them too. Thanks for visiting!
         <a class="pagelink" href="http://crazylittleprojects.com/about-me">
          [Read More ]
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>

   jQuery(function ($) {

	var id = "6840";

	var uniq_id = "55a48994f0532";

	var submit_url = "http://crazylittleprojects.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=wpp_store_email";

	var options = {"enabled":true,"theme":"default_theme","delay_time":"500","mask_color":"#c9c9c7","border_color":"#18a2cb","transition":"elastic","rules":{"show_on_homepage":true,"show_to_logged_in_users":true,"hide_on_mobile_devices":true,"use_cookies":true,"cookie_expiration_time":"15","show_only_on_homepage":false,"show_only_to_search_engine_visitors":false,"exit_popup":false,"when_post_end_rule":false}};

	var rules = options.rules;
	
	if ( ! wpp_check_rules( rules, id ) )
		return false;

	var do_popup_function = function() {
		$.colorbox({
			inline: true,
			fixed: true,
			width: "450px",
			href: "#default_theme-auto_popup-6840",
			className: 'cbox_wpp_default_theme',
			overlayClose: false,
			escKey: false,
			transition: options.transition,
			

			/*onOpen: function() {
				$("#colorbox").css("opacity", 0);
			},

			onComplete: function() {
				$("#colorbox").css("opacity", 1);
			},*/

			onClosed: function() {

				if ( rules.use_cookies )
					wpp_place_popup_close_cookie( id, rules.cookie_expiration_time );
			}
		});

		$('#cboxOverlay.cbox_wpp_default_theme').css( 'background', options.mask_color );

		$('.cbox_wpp_default_theme #cboxLoadedContent').css( 'border-color', options.border_color );

		//$('#cboxOverlay.cbox_wpp_default_theme').css( 'opacity', 0.8 );

	
	};

	if ( rules.exit_popup ) {

		wpp_do_exit_popup( do_popup_function );

	} else if ( rules.when_post_end_rule ) {

		wpp_check_when_post_rule( do_popup_function );

	} else {

		setTimeout( do_popup_function, options.delay_time );
	
	}


	if ( rules.comment_autofill ) {
		
		wpp_do_comment_autofill( uniq_id, 'af1239431f69d0a6faad33a1df46d8d9' );
	
	}

	$('.' + uniq_id + ' input[type=submit]' ).click(function(e){
		e.preventDefault();

		wpp_handle_form_submit( id, uniq_id, submit_url, rules.cookie_expiration_time );
	});

});
  </script>
